namespace = spleasure


## BE WARNED, there's some creepy stuff here. And the cold and crude language of coding will make it look even more nasty.

#spleasure.1 umbrella event
#spleasure.2-56 temptation events
#spleasure.57-67 mutation events
#spleasure.90-91 hide Deformitiy
#spleasure 68-89 don't remember

#spleasure.92-15905 Quirking Events

#spleasure.160-X Polymorph Events

#NEVER USE A SUSPICIOUS EVENT_IMAGE FOR THE TEMPTATION EVENT. THE PLAYER MUST NOT KNOW WHAT'S HE'S GETTING INTO.
##THE CHARACTER IS PRIMED BY A TEMPTATION EVENT WHEN HE GAINS THE SPIRITUALLYTEMPTED_SLAANESH/PHYSICALLYTEMPTED_SLAANESH FLAG.
#Once he has the flag, another umbrella event is activated to determine what happens when a courtiers nag him (at that point, depending on the choice, the character becomes a full cultist, gains the proper flag and unlocks the targetted decision).

#MAIN FLAGS IN USE:
## elf_slaaneshi_cultist
## spirituallytempted_slaanesh
## physicallytempted_slaanesh

###################################################

### Umbrella event (called on_action) for spontaneous conversion

character_event = {
	id = spleasure.1
	hide_window = yes

	only_rulers = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { higher_tier_than = BARON
			age = 40		#elves
			NOT = { society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure  }
		  NOT = { has_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh }
		  NOT = { has_character_flag = physicallytempted_slaanesh }
		  NOT = { trait = malekith }
		  NOT = { trait = everqueen }
		  NOT = { has_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion }
		trait = creature_elf
		NOT = { religion = cult_of_pleasure
			religion = atharti }
		OR = { religion = cadai
			religion = cytharai }
		OR = { trait = scholar
			trait = poet
			trait = mystic
			trait = brilliant
			trait = quick
			trait = genius
			trait = hedonist
			trait = gluttonous
			trait = drunkard
			trait = cruel
			trait = impaler
			trait = temperate
			trait = chaste
			trait = celibate }
		}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.75
			ai = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			ai = no
			has_focus = focus_seduction
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = stressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = depressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = is_fat
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = is_malnourished
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = addict
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = seducer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = seductress
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = theologian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = isolationist_elf
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			k_avelorn = { holder_scope = { trait = everqueen
							society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			k_avelorn = { holder_scope = { trait = everqueen
							religion = cult_of_pleasure } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cytharai
			religion_authority = 0.50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cytharai
			religion_authority = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cadai
			religion_authority = 0.25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cadai
			religion_authority = 0.50
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
				#Spiritual call
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_poet }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = poet } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.2 }
					}
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_scholar }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = scholar } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.15 }
					}
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_mystic }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = mystic } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.22 }
					}
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_genius }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = bright }
							NOT = { trait = smart }
							NOT = { trait = quick }
							NOT = { trait = brilliant }
							NOT = { trait = genius } }
					long_character_event = { id = spleasure.27 }
					}
				#Physical call
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = hedonist }
							NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
							NOT = { trait = temperate } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.32 }
					}
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_drunkard }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = hedonist }
							NOT = { trait = drunkard }
							NOT = { trait = temperate } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.39 }
					}
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = lustful }
							NOT = { trait = chaste }
							NOT = { trait = celibate } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.46 }
					}
				20 = {
					modifier = { factor = 0
							has_character_flag = temptation_won_cruel }
					modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = cruel }
							NOT = { trait = kind }
							NOT = { trait = impaler } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.51 }
					}


			} #closesrandomlist
		} #closesimmediate
}
# Poet has lost inspiration
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.2
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	desc = { text = EVTDESCA_spleasure2
		trigger = { religion_group = cadai_group }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCB_spleasure2
		trigger = { religion_group = cytharai_group }
		}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure2 # Use stuff
		character_event = { id = spleasure.3 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure2 # Cut yourself
		character_event = { id = spleasure.4 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure2 # No thanks
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_poet
		ai_chance = { factor = 98 }
	}
}
# Poet - A
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.3
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	desc = { text = EVTDESCA_spleasure3
		trigger = { religion_group = cadai_group }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCB_spleasure3
		trigger = { religion_group = cytharai_group }
		}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure3
		set_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		add_trait = addict
		hidden_tooltip = { random_list = { 40 = { character_event = { id = spleasure.5 } }
						30 = { character_event = { id = spleasure.6 } }
						25 = { character_event = { id = spleasure.7 } }
						5 = { character_event = { id = spleasure.8 } }	 # Tripping events
					}
				}
	}
}
# Poet - B
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.4
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	desc = { text = EVTDESCA_spleasure4
		trigger = { religion_group = cadai_group }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCB_spleasure4
		trigger = { religion_group = cytharai_group }
		}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure4
		set_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		add_trait = wounded
		change_learning = 1
		long_character_event = { id = spleasure.12 days = 20 random = 60 }
	}
}


# Tripping event 1
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.5
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_demons
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure5

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure5
		change_learning = 1
		if = { limit = { NOT = { trait = paranoid } }
			add_trait = paranoid }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.9 days = 45 random = 50 }
	}
}

# Tripping event 4
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.8
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_demons
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure8

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure8
		if = { limit = { trait = brilliant }
			remove_trait = brilliant
			add_trait = genius }
		if = { limit = { trait = quick }
			remove_trait = quick
			add_trait = brilliant }
		if = { limit = { trait = smart }
			remove_trait = smart
			add_trait = quick }
		if = { limit = { trait = bright }
			remove_trait = bright
			add_trait = smart }
		if = { limit = {
				NOT = { trait = bright }
				NOT = { trait = smart }
				NOT = { trait = quick }
				NOT = { trait = brilliant }
				NOT = { trait = genius } }
			add_trait = bright }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.9 days = 45 random = 50 }
	}
}

# Servant making problems
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.9
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure9

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure9	#Have him join you
		character_event = { id = spleasure.10 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure9	#Kill him of overdose
		character_event = { id = spleasure.11 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure9	#Stop
		clr_character_flag =  spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_poet
		random_list = { 80 = {  }
				20 = { remove_trait = addict } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
	}
}

# Genius - A
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.28
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure28
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure28
		if = { limit = { NOT = { trait = proud } }
			add_trait = proud }
		set_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		character_event = { id = spleasure.30 days = 5 random = 10 }
	}
}

	}

# Gluttonous/Temperate event
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.32
	picture = GFX_evt_feast

	desc = { text = EVTDESCA_spleasure32
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				trait = gluttonous }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCB_spleasure32
		trigger = { is_female = no
				trait = gluttonous }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCC_spleasure32
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				trait = temperate }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCD_spleasure32
		trigger = { is_female = no
				trait = temperate }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCE_spleasure32
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous } }
		}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure32 # They're wrong, I'm fine!
		trigger = { trait = gluttonous }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.33 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure32 # Maybe a little moderation?
		trigger = { trait = gluttonous }
		random_list = { 60 = {  }
				40 = { remove_trait = gluttonous } }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
		ai_chance = { factor = 98 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure32 # I little indulgement won't hurt...
		trigger = { trait = temperate }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.34 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDspleasure32 # No thanks
		trigger = { trait = temperate }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
		ai_chance = { factor = 98 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEspleasure32 # What's wrong with having some fun?
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous } }
		random_list = { 60 = {  }
				20 = { add_trait = drunkard }
				20 = { add_trait = gluttonous } }
		long_character_event = { id = spleasure.35 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFspleasure32 # Let's keep it classy
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous } }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
		ai_chance = { factor = 98 }
	}
}

# Lustful/chaste event
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.46
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers

	desc = { text = EVTDESCA_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				religion_group = cadai_group
				trait = lustful }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCB_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = no
				religion_group = cadai_group
				trait = lustful }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCC_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				religion_group = cytharai_group
				trait = lustful }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCD_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = no
				religion_group = cytharai_group
				trait = lustful }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCE_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				religion_group = cadai_group
				NOT = { trait = lustful } }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCF_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = no
				religion_group = cadai_group
				NOT = { trait = lustful } }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCG_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				religion_group = cytharai_group
				NOT = { trait = lustful } }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCH_spleasure46
		trigger = { is_female = no
				religion_group = cytharai_group
				NOT = { trait = lustful } }
		}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure46 # Huuh! Kinky!
		trigger = { trait = lustful }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.47 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure46 # That's not really my sort of things...
		trigger = { trait = lustful }
		random_list = { 60 = {  }
				40 = { remove_trait = lustful } }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful
		ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEspleasure46 # Maybe.. just this once?
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
		if = { limit = { trait = celibate }
			remove_trait = celibate }
		random_list = { 60 = {  }
				40 = { add_trait = lustful } }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.49 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFspleasure46 # How dare you!
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful
		ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
	}
}

# Cruel/Kind event, clumsy servant
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.51
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	desc = { text = EVTDESCA_spleasure51
		trigger = { OR = { trait = impaler
				trait = cruel }
				religion_group = cytharai_group }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCB_spleasure51
		trigger = { OR = { trait = impaler
				trait = cruel }
				religion_group = cadai_group }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCC_spleasure51
		trigger = { trait = kind
				religion_group = cytharai_group }
		}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCD_spleasure51
		trigger = { trait = kind
				religion_group = cadai_group }
		}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure51 # You miserable wretch!
		trigger = { OR = { trait = impaler
				trait = cruel } }
		random_list = { 70 = {  }
				30 = { add_trait = wroth } }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.52 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure51 # You know what? He's beneath me.
		trigger = { OR = { trait = impaler
				trait = cruel } }
		random_list = { 60 = {  }
				40 = { remove_trait = cruel } }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_cruel
		ai_chance = { factor = 98 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEspleasure51 # That's it! Now you're getting it!
		trigger = { trait = kind }
		random_list = { 60 = {  }
				40 = { remove_trait = kind } }
		character_event = { id = spleasure.54 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFspleasure51 # Don't worry, I can manage...
		trigger = { trait = kind }
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_cruel
		ai_chance = { factor = 98 }
	}
}

##################MUTATION EVENTS###############

# The character did some nasty thing, he receives a gift from the Dark Prince
# Umbrella event
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.57
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
				#Tongue
				#Horns
				#Beauty
				#Ugliness
				#Madness
				#Gender swap
				35 = { 	modifier = { factor = 0.5
							trait = creature_elf }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.5705 } }
				30 = {  modifier = { factor = 0.5
							trait = creature_elf }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.58 } }
				10 = {  modifier = { factor = 0.5
							trait = creature_elf }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.59 } }
				10 = {  modifier = { factor = 0.5
							trait = creature_elf }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.60 } }
				5 = { character_event = { id = spleasure.61 } }
				5 = { modifier = { factor = 0
							NOT = { trait = creature_elf }
							NOT = { trait = creature_human }
							NOT = { trait = creature_halfling }
							NOT = { trait = creature_dwarf }
							NOT = { trait = creature_chaos_dwarf }
							NOT = { trait = creature_amazon }
							NOT = { trait = creature_beastman } }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.171 } }
			} #closesrandomlist

	}
}


# Mutation - Tongue
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.5705
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure57

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure57	#hide it with magic
		trigger = { OR = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_4 } }
		random_list = {
				50 = { 	modifier = { factor = 0.75
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1 }
					modifier = { factor = 1.25
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2 }
					modifier = { factor = 1.5
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3 }
					modifier = { factor = 1.75
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4 }
					modifier = { factor = 0.75
							has_character_flag = hidden_mutation }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.62 days = 15 random = 23 } }	#Success
				50 = {
					character_event = { id = spleasure.63 days = 15 random = 24 } }	#Failure
			} #closesrandomlist


	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure57	#hide it with intrigue
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		random_list = {
				40 = { 	modifier = { factor = 0.75
							NOT = { intrigue = 10 } }
					modifier = { factor = 1.25
							intrigue = 10 }
					modifier = { factor = 1.5
							intrigue = 15 }
					modifier = { factor = 1.75
							intrigue = 20 }
					modifier = { factor = 0.75
							has_character_flag = hidden_mutation }
					character_event = { id = spleasure.62 days = 15 random = 23 } }	#Success
				60 = {
					character_event = { id = spleasure.63 days = 15 random = 24 } }	#Failure
			} #closesrandomlist


	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure57
		add_trait = piercing_tongue
		change_variable = { which = "mutation_counter" value = 1 }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { religion = atharti
					religion = cult_of_pleasure
					religion = slaanesh } }
			#character_event = { id = spleasure.65 } 	#cultist exposed only when hidden
			increase_visibility_effect = yes # increase visibility
		}

	}
}

# Mutation - Beauty
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.59
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure59

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure59
		change_variable = { which = "mutation_counter" value = 1 }
		if = { limit = { trait = pretty }
			remove_trait = pretty
			add_trait = beautiful }
		if = { limit = { trait = fair }
			remove_trait = fair
			add_trait = pretty }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { trait = beautiful
					trait = pretty
					trait = fair }
				OR = { trait = plain
					trait = ugly
					trait = unsightly } }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = plain
				 remove_trait = ugly
				remove_trait = unsightly }
			add_trait = fair }

	}
}

			add_trait = unsightly }
		if = { limit = { trait = plain }

			add_trait = ugly }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { trait = ugly
					trait = plain
					trait = unsightly }
				OR = { trait = pretty
					trait = beautiful
					trait = fair } }
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = pretty

				remove_trait = beautiful }
			add_trait = plain }

	}

		any_vassal = { character_event = { id = spleasure.66 days = 1 } }
		if = { limit = { independent = no }
			liege = { character_event = { id = spleasure.67 days = 1 } } }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = spleasure.69
	desc = EVTDESCspleasure.69
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cultist

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure.69			# Toy with his mind
	trigger = { OR = { has_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
						society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure}}
	hidden_tooltip = { random_list = {
						50 = { FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.79 days = 10 random = 15 } } }
						50 = { FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.76 days = 10 random = 15 } } }
					}
		 	}
	}
	option = { name = EVTOPTBspleasure.69			# Shame him
	trigger = { has_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh }
			hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.70 } } }
	}

	option = { name = EVTOPTCspleasure.69			# Tease his cravings
	trigger = {
		OR = {
		has_character_flag = physicallytempted_slaanesh
		society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure
		}
	}
	hidden_tooltip = { random_list = {
						80 = { FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.82 days = 10 random = 15 } } }
						20 = { FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.85 days = 10 random = 15 } } }
					}
		 	}
	}
	option = { name = EVTOPTDspleasure.69			# Enflame his lust
	trigger = {
		OR = {
		has_character_flag = physicallytempted_slaanesh
		society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure
		}
	}
			hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.87 days = 10 random = 15 } } }
	}

	option = { name = EVTOPTEspleasure.69			# Changed my mind
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_twisting
				}
					FROM = { opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_twisted
							years = 1 }
						}
	}

}

	id = spleasure.76
	desc = "EVTDESC1016"
	picture = "GFX_evt_lunatic"
	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1016"
		hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = paranoid 		#cheating cultist
				FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.77 } }	#notify and choose what to do
				 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cynical
				NOT = {
					trait = charitable
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45

				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38275 #Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = charitable
				NOT = {
					trait = cynical
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10

				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38275 #Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = cynical
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = charitable
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22

				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38275 #Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cynical
				trait = charitable
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22

				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38275 #Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1016"
		hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.78 } }	#notify and choose what to do
				 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gregarious
				NOT = {
					trait = deceitful
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45

				add_trait = trusting
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38250 #Notify Trusting
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = deceitful
				NOT = {
					trait = gregarious
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10

				add_trait = trusting
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38250 #Notify Trusting
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = gregarious
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = deceitful
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22

				add_trait = trusting
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38250 #Notify Trusting
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gregarious
				trait = deceitful
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22

				add_trait = trusting
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38250 #Notify Trusting
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

character_event = {
	id = spleasure.85
	desc = EVTDESC65040
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	hide_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA65040
		add_trait = drunkard
		hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.86 } }	#notify and choose what to do
				 }

	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB65040
		hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.83 } }	#notify and choose what to do
				 }
		if = {
			limit = { trait = gluttonous }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dlc = "Reapers"
						}
					}
					add_trait = ill
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Reapers"
					}
					add_food_poisoning_symptom_effect = yes
				}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = gluttonous } }
			add_trait = gluttonous
		}
	}
}

				hidden_tooltip = {

						id = 38274 #Notify Chaste
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
				NOT = {
					trait = arbitrary
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22

				add_trait = chaste
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38274 #Notify Chaste
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = proud
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22

				add_trait = chaste
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38274 #Notify Chaste
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Hiding disfigurement spell
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.90
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure90
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
				trait = mut_doublehead
				trait = mut_beak
				trait = mut_teeth
				trait = mut_eyes
				trait = mut_bigeyes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { 
		text = EVTDESCBspleasure90
		trigger = { 
			NOR = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
				trait = mut_doublehead
				trait = mut_beak
				trait = mut_teeth
				trait = mut_eyes
				trait = mut_bigeyes
			}
			OR = { 
				trait = disfigured
				trait = scarred 
				trait = scarred_mid
				trait = scarred_high
			} 
		} 
	}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCCspleasure90
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
				trait = mut_doublehead
				trait = mut_beak
				trait = mut_teeth
				trait = mut_eyes
				trait = mut_bigeyes
				trait = disfigured 
				trait = scarred
			}
			trait = is_fat 
		} 
	}
	desc = { text = EVTDESCDspleasure90
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
				trait = mut_doublehead
				trait = mut_beak
				trait = mut_teeth
				trait = mut_eyes
				trait = mut_bigeyes
				trait = disfigured 
				trait = scarred
			}
		
			trait = is_malnourished 
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure90
		if = { 
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = mut_doublehead
					trait = mut_beak
					trait = mut_bigeyes
					trait = mut_horns
					trait = mut_thirdeye
					trait = mut_spines
					trait = mut_scales
					trait = mut_tongue
					trait = mut_crests
					trait = mut_teeth
					trait = mut_eyes
				}
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_mut_slaanesh } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_fat } 
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_doublehead }
				remove_trait = mut_doublehead
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_bigeyes }
				remove_trait = mut_bigeyes
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_beak }
				remove_trait = mut_beak
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_horns }
				remove_trait = mut_horns
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_thirdeye }
				remove_trait = mut_thirdeye
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_spines }
				remove_trait = mut_spines
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_scales }
				remove_trait = mut_scales
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_tongue }
				remove_trait = mut_tongue
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_crests }
				remove_trait = mut_crests
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_teeth }
				remove_trait = mut_teeth
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = mut_eyes }
				remove_trait = mut_eyes
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_mut_slaanesh
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes 
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				trait = is_malnourished
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_disfigurement } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_fat } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_mut_slaanesh }
			}
			remove_trait = is_malnourished
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_undernourished
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes 
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				trait = is_fat
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_disfigurement } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished } 
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = hidden_fat } 
			}
			remove_trait = is_fat
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = hidden_fat
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes 
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = { 
					trait = disfigured
					trait = scarred 
					trait = scarred_mid
					trait = scarred_high
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { trait = disfigured }
				remove_trait = disfigured
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = scarred_high }
				remove_trait = scarred_high
				add_trait = scarred_mid
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { trait = scarred_mid }
				remove_trait = scarred_mid
				add_trait = scarred
			}
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = hidden_disfigurement
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes 
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = { 
				60 = {
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.25
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.5
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.75
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 2.25
						trait = genius
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 2.0
						trait = brilliant
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.5
						trait = quick
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.25
						trait = smart
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.1
						trait = smart
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.1
						learning = 12
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.1
						learning = 14
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.1
						learning = 16
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.1
						learning = 18
					}
				}
				40 = {	#Backfire
					modifier = { 
						factor = 0
						is_doom_very_low_trigger = yes
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 2
						NOT = { learning = 12 }
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 2
						is_doom_low_trigger = yes
					}
					character_event = { id = spleasure.91 days = 150 random = 133 } 
				} 
			}
		}
	}
}

#Set integrity variable
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.96
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
       if = {
           limit = { OR = { trait = creature_human
                    trait = creature_amazon } }
		set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 2 }
      		}
       if = {
           limit = { trait = creature_elf }
		set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 3 }
      		}
       if = {
           limit = { trait = creature_dwarf }
		set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 4 }
      		}
       if = {
           limit = { trait = creature_chaos_dwarf }
		set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 }
      		}
       if = {
           limit = { trait = everqueen }
		change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 9 }
      		}
       if = {
           limit = { trait = phoenix_king }
		change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 7 }
      		}
       if = {
           limit = { trait = avatar_kurnous }
		change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 }
      		}

           limit = { trait = avatar_isha }
		change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 }
      		}

		change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 3 }
      		}

				trait = vampire_carstein_visible

# The target was tempted, decide the improvement
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.99003
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure99003
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = refused_tempt_start } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure99003
		trigger = { has_character_flag = refused_tempt_start } }
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure99003 #Too chaste
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = refused_tempt_start
			character_event = { id = spleasure.130 days = 5 random = 25 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 34
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					FROM = { trait = lustful }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = lustful
					}
				}
		}
	option = { name = EVTOPTBspleasure99003 #Too modest
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = refused_tempt_start
			character_event = { id = spleasure.140 days = 5 random = 25 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 33
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					FROM = { OR = { trait = proud
							trait = ambitious
							trait = lunatic_3
							trait = lunatic_2
							trait = envious } }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = proud
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = gregarious
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = diligent
					}
				}
		}
	option = { name = EVTOPTCspleasure99003 #Too serious
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = refused_tempt_start
			character_event = { id = spleasure.150 days = 5 random = 25 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 33
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					FROM = { OR = { trait = hedonist
							trait = addict
							trait = drunkard } }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = hedonist
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = drunkard
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = addict
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = gregarious
					}
				 }
		}
}

# Too plain (integrity gives flavor as to how the character feels about it, rather than how much they are virtuous in general)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.100
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure100
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 10 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCCspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 10 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCDspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCEspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 25 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCFspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 25 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 30 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCGspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 30 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 40 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCHspleasure100
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 40 } } }

	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure100 #Agree
		random_list = { 50 = { change_diplomacy = 1
					set_character_flag = fake_skill_s }
				50 = {  }
				 }
		hidden_tooltip = { if = { limit = { has_character_flag = fake_skill_s } 	#Slaanesh rigs the game for your enjoyment
					random_list = { 99 = { change_diplomacy = -1
								clr_character_flag = fake_skill_s }
								1 = { clr_character_flag = fake_skill_s }
				 			}
					}
				 }
				hidden_tooltip = { random_list = { 50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = -5 } }
								50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = -3 } }
								 }
						 }
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.101 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 20
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = proud
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = plain
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = ugly
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = unsightly
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = envious
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = shy
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = deceitful }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = slaanesh_demon }
					}
				}
		}
	option = { name = EVTOPTBspleasure100 #Refuse
		prestige = -50
				hidden_tooltip = { random_list = { 50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 5 } }
								50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 3 } }
								 }
						 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 } }
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.101 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 80
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = humble
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = pretty
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = gregarious
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = fair
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = beautiful
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = content
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = honest }
					}
				 }
		}

}
# Too plain - overview (accepted/refused)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.101
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure101
		trigger = { NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 } }
				NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 10 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCCspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 10 } }
				NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCDspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 } }
				NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCEspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 } }
				NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 25 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCFspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 25 } }
				NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 30 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCGspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 30 } }
				NOT = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 40 } } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCHspleasure101
		trigger = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 40 } } } }

	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure101
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.102 days = 10 random = 30 } }		#flatter (works better for proud)

		ai_chance = { factor = 34
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = deceitful
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25

					}

					factor = 1.25
					trait = smart
					}
				modifier = {

					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = genius
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = quick
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { OR = { trait = dim
							trait = slow
							trait = idiot
							trait = imbecile } }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = proud }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					FROM = { trait = gregarious }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					FROM = { trait = hedonist }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					FROM = { OR = { trait = fair
							trait = beautiful
							trait = pretty } }
					}
				}
	}
	option = { name = EVTOPTBspleasure101
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.103 days = 10 random = 30 } }		#shame (works better for insecure)

		ai_chance = { factor = 33
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = deceitful
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = gregarious
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = paranoid
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = envious
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = cruel
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = arbitrary
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { OR = { trait = dim
							trait = slow
							trait = idiot
							trait = imbecile } }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = trusting }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					FROM = { trait = shy }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					FROM = { trait = humble }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					FROM = { OR = { trait = plain
							trait = ugly
							trait = unsightly } }
					}
				}
	}
	option = { name = EVTOPTCspleasure101
		trigger = { OR = { trait = slaanesh_demon
					is_liege_of = FROM } }
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.104 days = 10 random = 30 } }		#reprimand (works better for virtuous)

		ai_chance = { factor = 33
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = honest
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = wroth
					}
				modifier = {

					trait = cruel
					}
				modifier = {

					}

					factor = 1.25
					trait = arbitrary
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { OR = { trait = quick
							trait = smart
							trait = brilliant
							trait = genius } }

				modifier = {

# Too plain - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.106
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
				random_list= {
						50 = {
							FROM = { add_trait = scarred
								character_event = { id = spleasure.107 days = 1 } }
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								trait = scarred
								}
							}
						30 = {  FROM = { add_trait = disfigured
								character_event = { id = spleasure.108 days = 1 } }
							 }
						20 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								FROM = { trait = beautiful }
								}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								FROM = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_1 }
									NOT = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_2 }
									NOT = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_3 }
									NOT = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_4 } }
								}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.75
								FROM = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_1 }
								}
							modifier = {
								factor = 1.5
								FROM = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_2 }
								}
							modifier = {
								factor = 2
								FROM = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_3 }
								}
							modifier = {
								factor = 3
								FROM = { has_character_modifier = magic_power_4 }
								}
							FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.109 days = 1 }

								if = {
									limit = { trait = pretty }
										remove_trait = pretty
										add_trait = beautiful
										}
								if = {
									limit = { trait = fair }
										remove_trait = fair
										add_trait = pretty
										}
								if = {
									limit = {
										NOT = { trait = beautiful }
										NOT = { trait = pretty }
										NOT = { trait = fair }
										NOT = { trait = plain }
										NOT = { trait = ugly }
										NOT = { trait = unsightly }
										}
										add_trait = fair
									}
								if = {
									limit = { trait = plain }
									remove_trait = plain
									}
								if = {
									limit = { trait = ugly }
									remove_trait = ugly
									add_trait = plain
									}
								if = {
									limit = { trait = unsightly }
									remove_trait = unsightly
									add_trait = ugly
									}
								} #closes 20
	 						} #closes randomlist
						} #closes from
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}
		}
}

# Too thin - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.116
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}
							FROM = {
								if = {
									limit = { trait = is_fat }
										character_event = { id = spleasure.119 days = 20 random = 30 }
										}
								if = {
									limit = {
										NOT = { trait = is_fat }
										NOT = { trait = is_malnourished }
										}
										character_event = { id = spleasure.118 days = 20 random = 30 }
									}
								if = {
									limit = { trait = is_malnourished }
									remove_trait = is_malnourished
										character_event = { id = spleasure.117 days = 20 random = 30 }
									}
						} #closes from
		}
}

	id = spleasure.125
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure125
		trigger = { FROM = { NOT = { is_female = yes } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure125
		trigger = { FROM = { is_female = yes } } }
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure125
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

# Too fat - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.126
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}
							FROM = {
								if = {
									limit = { trait = is_malnourished }
										character_event = { id = spleasure.129 days = 20 random = 30 }
										}
								if = {
									limit = {
										NOT = { trait = is_fat }
										NOT = { trait = is_malnourished }
										}
										character_event = { id = spleasure.128 days = 20 random = 30 }
									}
								if = {
									limit = { trait = is_fat }
										character_event = { id = spleasure.127 days = 20 random = 30 }
									}
						} #closes from
		}
}

# Too chaste (integrity gives flavor as to how the character feels about it, rather than how much they are virtuous in general)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.130
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure130
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 10 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCCspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 10 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCDspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 15 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCEspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 20 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 25 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCFspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 25 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 30 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCGspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 30 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 40 } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCHspleasure130
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 40 } } }

	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cultist

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure130 #Agree
		random_list = { 50 = { change_diplomacy = 1
					set_character_flag = fake_skill_s }
				50 = {  }
				 }
		hidden_tooltip = { if = { limit = { has_character_flag = fake_skill_s } 	#Slaanesh rigs the game for your enjoyment
					random_list = { 99 = { change_diplomacy = -1
								clr_character_flag = fake_skill_s }
								1 = { clr_character_flag = fake_skill_s }
				 			}
					}
				 }
				hidden_tooltip = { random_list = { 50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = -5 } }
								50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = -3 } }
								 }
						 }
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.131 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 20
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = lustful
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = greedy
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = humble
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = hedonist
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = gregarious
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = drunkard
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = deceitful }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = slaanesh_demon }
					}
				}
		}
	option = { name = EVTOPTBspleasure130 #Refuse
		prestige = -50
				hidden_tooltip = { random_list = { 50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 5 } }
								50 = { change_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 3 } }
								 }
						 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 1 } }
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.131 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 80
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					trait = proud
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = celibate
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = chaste
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = shy
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = { trait = honest }
					}
				 }
		}

}

character_event = {
	id = spleasure.135
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure135
		trigger = { FROM = { NOT = { is_female = yes } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure135
		trigger = { FROM = { is_female = yes } } }
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure135
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

# Too Chaste - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.136
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}
				random_list= {
						50 = {
							FROM = { remove_trait = celibate
								remove_trait = chaste
								add_trait = lustful
								character_event = { id = spleasure.137 days = 1 } }
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								trait = lustful
								}
							}
							30 = {
								modifier = {
									factor = 0
									FROM = { trait = cruel }
					            }
								FROM = {
									remove_trait = kind
									add_trait = cruel
									character_event = { id = spleasure.138 days = 1 }
					    		}
					        }
						20 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								NOT = { trait = lustful }
								}
							FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.139 days = 1 }
								add_trait = depressed
								} #closes 20
	 						} #closes randomlist
						} #closes from
		}
}

	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure145
		trigger = { FROM = { is_female = yes } } }
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure145
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

# Too Modest - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.146
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}
				random_list= {
						50 = {
							FROM = {
								remove_trait = humble
								add_trait = proud
								character_event = { id = spleasure.147 days = 1 } }
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								trait = proud
								}
							}
						30 = {  FROM = { remove_trait = content
								add_trait = ambitious
								character_event = { id = spleasure.148 days = 1 } }
							 }
						20 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								trait = proud
								}
							FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.149 days = 1 }
								remove_trait = kind
								add_trait = envious
								} #closes 20
	 						} #closes randomlist
						} #closes from
		}
}

		trigger = { FROM = { is_female = yes } } }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure155
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

# Too Serious - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.156
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
	 	remove_opinion = { who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_quirking
				}
					FROM = {
						set_variable = { which = "s_integrity" value = 0 }
						opinion = { who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
							years = 1 }
						}
				random_list= {
						50 = {
							FROM = {
								remove_trait = temperate
								add_trait = drunkard
								character_event = { id = spleasure.157 days = 1 } }
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								trait = drunkard
								}
							}
						30 = {  FROM = { remove_trait = temperate
								add_trait = hedonist
								character_event = { id = spleasure.158 days = 1 } }
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								trait = hedonist
								}
							 }
						20 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								NOT = { trait = drunkard }
								}
							FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.159 days = 1 }
								remove_trait = temperate
								add_trait = addict
								} #closesFROM
	 						} #closes 20
						} #closes randomlist
		}
}

# The prisoner becomes monstrous
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.161
	desc = EVTDESCAspleasure161
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure161
		set_graphical_culture = beastman_ungor
		add_trait = monstrous
		prisoner = no
		opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_me
				who = FROM }
		hidden_tooltip = {
					FROM = { any_vassal = { limit = { religion = cadai }
								opinion = { modifier = opinion_barbaric
										who = FROM }
									} #closes anyvassal
								} #closes from
				any_dynasty_member = { limit = { religion_group = cytharai_group }
							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family_druchii
								who = FROM }
							} #closes anydynastyme
				any_dynasty_member = { limit = { NOT = { religion_group = cytharai_group } }
							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family
								who = FROM }
							} #closes anydynastyme
					}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.16105 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

# The prisoner becomes monstrous - Notify jailer
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.16105
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure16105
		trigger = { FROM = { NOT = { is_female = yes } } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure16105
		trigger = { FROM = { is_female = yes } } }
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure16105
		any_vassal = { limit = { NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { trait = quick }
					NOT = { trait = genius }
					}
				opinion = { modifier = opinion_scared_into_submission
						who = ROOT }
			 }
		any_courtier = { limit = { NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { trait = quick }
					NOT = { trait = genius }
					}
				opinion = { modifier = opinion_scared_into_submission
						who = ROOT }
			 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family_druchii

							} #closes anydynastyme

							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family
								who = FROM }

							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family
								who = FROM }
							} #closes anydynastyme
				}

		}

# The prisoner switches gender
long_character_event = {
	id = spleasure.169
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure169
		trigger = { NOT = { is_female = yes }
			 OR = { trait = creature_human
				trait = creature_halfling } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure169
		trigger = { is_female = yes
			 OR = { trait = creature_human
				trait = creature_halfling } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCCspleasure169
		trigger = { NOT = { is_female = yes }
			 OR = { trait = creature_dwarf
				trait = creature_chaos_dwarf } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCDspleasure169
		trigger = { is_female = yes
			 OR = { trait = creature_dwarf
				trait = creature_chaos_dwarf } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCEspleasure169
		trigger = { NOT = { is_female = yes }
				trait = creature_elf } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCFspleasure169
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				trait = creature_elf } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCGspleasure169
		trigger = { NOT = { is_female = yes }
				trait = creature_beastman } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCHspleasure169
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				trait = creature_beastman } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCIspleasure169
		trigger = { NOT = { is_female = yes }
				trait = creature_amazon } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCLspleasure169
		trigger = { is_female = yes
				trait = creature_amazon } }

	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure169
		set_gender = opposite
		add_trait = transgender
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_trait = infertile
		}
		if = { limit = { trait = homosexual }
		remove_trait = homosexual
		}
		else_if = { limit = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
		add_trait = homosexual
		}
		if = { limit = { trait = creature_beastman
				is_female = yes }
				add_trait = horns_small }
		if = { limit = { trait = creature_beastman
				is_female = no }
				remove_trait = horns_small
				remove_trait = horns_average
				remove_trait = horns_big
				add_trait = horns_none }
		opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_me
				who = FROM }
		hidden_tooltip = {
					FROM = { any_vassal = { limit = { religion = cadai }
								opinion = { modifier = opinion_barbaric
										who = FROM }
									} #closes anyvassal
								} #closes from
				any_dynasty_member = { limit = { religion_group = cytharai_group }
							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family_druchii
								who = FROM }
							} #closes anydynastyme
				any_dynasty_member = { limit = { NOT = { religion_group = cytharai_group } }
							opinion = { modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family
								who = FROM }
							} #closes anydynastyme
				}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = spleasure.16905 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

		}

#The swap is complete (straight), notify spouse
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.173
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAspleasure173
		trigger = { NOT = { is_female = yes } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBspleasure173
		trigger = { is_female = yes } }
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { name = EVTOPTAspleasure173
		trigger = { OR = { trait = homosexual
					ai = no } } #A wish come true
		hidden_tooltip = { spouse = { character_event = { id = spleasure.17305 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
	option = { name = EVTOPTBspleasure173
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } } #This marriage is over
		hidden_tooltip = { spouse = { character_event = { id = spleasure.17306 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
	option = { name = EVTOPTCspleasure173
		trigger = { ai = no } #I don't care
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		}
}

#Gender-swapped woman knocks up by spouse
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.175
	# desc = EVTDESCspleasure175
	# picture = GFX_evt_cult_of_pleasure

	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_women = yes

	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
			trait = transgender
			NOT = { trait = creature_orc }		#Infertile species
			NOT = { trait = creature_goblin }
			NOT = { trait = creature_hobgoblin }
			NOT = { trait = creature_snotling }
			NOT = { trait = creature_nehekharan }
			is_vampire_trigger = no
		NOT = { trait = celibate }
		NOT = { trait = infertile }
		OR = { NOT = { age = 45 }
			AND = { NOT = { trait = creature_human }
				NOT = { trait = creature_halfling } } }
		is_pregnant = no
		spouse = {
			is_female = yes
			NOT = { trait = eunuch }
			NOT = { trait = creature_orc }		#Infertile species
			NOT = { trait = creature_goblin }
			NOT = { trait = creature_hobgoblin }
			NOT = { trait = creature_snotling }
			NOT = { trait = creature_nehekharan }
			is_vampire_trigger = no

			#To avoid halfbreeds
			OR = { AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_human }
						trait = creature_human }
				 AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_amazon }
						trait = creature_amazon }
				AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_elf }
						trait = creature_elf }
				AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_halfling }
						trait = creature_halfling }
				AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_dwarf }
						trait = creature_dwarf }
				AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_chaos_dwarf }
						trait = creature_chaos_dwarf }
				AND = { ROOT = { trait = creature_skaven }
						trait = creature_skaven }
				}

			is_alive = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = stage_progressed } #so that the consorts will cycle

		}
	}
